223. [Derive] Random derive normal 583: triple_product [derive_normal:triple_product]
================================================================================

2 imp
3 par

4

check

Output:

2 de
M: f: 1 auto
2 dir
3 trig
4 sub
5 pts
6 pf
7 div
Met: u: Method: Integration by parts
1. u = ln(x)^3
2. du/dx = 3*ln(x)^2/x
3. v = 9*x/ln(9)^3
4. I = u*v-Int[27*ln(x)^2/ln(9)^3] dx
